Firefox UserAgents 23rd July 2015


--------------------------------------------------------------
USE Infrastructure_Logs
GO
SET TRANSACTION ISOLATION LEVEL READ UNCOMMITTED;
--------------------------------------------------------------
SELECT UserAgent, COUNT(*) FROM dbo.tbZeusLogs (nolock)
WHERE 1=1
AND ClientIP NOT LIKE '10.%'
AND ClientIP NOT LIKE '127.0.0.1%'
AND ED >= DATEADD(MINUTE,-400,GETDATE()) 
AND UserAgent LIKE '%firefox%'
--------------------------------------------------------------
GROUP BY UserAgent
ORDER BY 2 DESC
